# Add FlagExists Method to ReadOnlyFlagStore Interface

**Repository:** flipt-io/flipt
**Access Scope:** You may modify files in `internal/`. You may read any file to understand existing patterns.

## Context

Flipt is a feature flag platform built with Go. The `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface defines the contract for reading flag data from storage backends. Multiple concrete types implement this interface across the codebase (filesystem snapshots, SQL backends, etc.).

The evaluation server needs a lightweight way to check if a flag exists without fetching the full flag object. Currently, it must call `GetFlag()` and check for errors, which is inefficient. A dedicated `FlagExists()` method would allow backends to optimize existence checks (e.g., via SQL `EXISTS` or filesystem stat).

## Task

Add a `FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req *flipt.GetFlagRequest) (bool, error)` method to the `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface and implement it in all concrete types that satisfy this interface.

**YOU MUST IMPLEMENT CODE CHANGES.**

### Requirements

1. **Find the interface definition** — Locate the `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface in the storage package and understand its existing methods (e.g., `GetFlag`, `ListFlags`, `CountFlags`)
2. **Find all implementations** — Search for all types that implement `ReadOnlyFlagStore`. These are types that have methods like `GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req *flipt.GetFlagRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error)` matching the interface
3. **Add the method to the interface** — Add `FlagExists` to the interface definition:
   ```go
   FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req *flipt.GetFlagRequest) (bool, error)
   ```
4. **Implement in each concrete type** — For each implementing type, add a `FlagExists` method that:
   - Takes `(ctx context.Context, req *flipt.GetFlagRequest) (bool, error)`
   - Calls the type's existing `GetFlag()` method
   - Returns `true, nil` if the flag is found
   - Returns `false, nil` if the flag is not found (not-found error)
   - Returns `false, err` for other errors
5. **Handle not-found errors** — Use the existing error patterns in each backend to distinguish "not found" from real errors. Look at how `GetFlag` callers handle the not-found case.

## Success Criteria

- `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface includes `FlagExists` method
- All concrete types that implement `ReadOnlyFlagStore` have a `FlagExists` method
- Each implementation correctly handles not-found vs real errors
- `go build ./internal/...` succeeds with zero errors
- No existing tests broken
- Changes are scoped to `internal/` only

     9→// e.g. cerr, match := errors.As[MyCustomError](err).
    10→func As[E error](err error) (e E, _ bool) {
    11→	return e, errors.As(err, &e)

    17→	_, match = As[E](err)
    18→	return
    19→}

    24→}

    28→	return E(fmt.Sprintf(format, args...))

    17→	// ErrNotImplemented is returned when a method has intentionally not been implemented
    18→	// This is usually reserved for the store write actions when the store is read-only
    19→	// but still needs to implement storage.Store
    20→	ErrNotImplemented = errors.New("not implemented")
    21→)
    22→
    23→// ReferencedSnapshotStore is a type which has a single function View.
    24→// View is a functional transaction interface for reading a snapshot
    25→// during the lifetime of a supplied function.
    26→type ReferencedSnapshotStore interface {
    27→	// View accepts a function which takes a storage.ReadOnlyStore (*StoreSnapshot).
    28→	// The ReferencedSnapshotStore will supply a snapshot which is valid
    29→	// for the lifetime of the provided function call.
    30→	// It expects a reference to be supplied on calls to View.
    31→	// Empty reference will be regarded as the default reference by the store.
    32→	View(context.Context, storage.Reference, func(storage.ReadOnlyStore) error) error
    33→	fmt.Stringer
    34→}
    35→
    36→// SnapshotStore is a type which has a single function View.
    37→// View is a functional transaction interface for reading a snapshot
    38→// during the lifetime of a supplied function.
    39→type SnapshotStore interface {
    40→	// View accepts a function which takes a storage.ReadOnlyStore (*SnapshotStore).
    41→	// The SnapshotStore will supply a snapshot which is valid
    42→	// for the lifetime of th
... (truncated)

package sql_test

import (

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"

func (s *DBTestSuite) TestGetFlag() {
	t := s.T()

	flag, err := s.store.CreateFlag(context.TODO(), &flipt.CreateFlagRequest{
		Key:         t.Name(),
		Name:        "foo",
		Description: "bar",
		Enabled:     true,
	})

	require.NoError(t, err)
	assert.NotNil(t, flag)

	got, err := s.store.GetFlag(context.TODO(), storage.NewResource(storage.DefaultNamespace, flag.Key))

	require.NoError(t, err)
	assert.NotNil(t, got)

	assert.Equal(t, storage.DefaultNamespace, got.NamespaceKey)
	assert.Equal(t, flag.Key, got.Key)
	assert.Equal(t, flag.Name, got.Name)
	assert.Equal(t, flag.Description, got.Description)
	assert.Equal(t, flag.Enabled, got.Enabled)
	assert.NotZero(t, flag.CreatedAt)
	assert.NotZero(t, flag.UpdatedAt)
}

	t := s.T()

   122→// FlagExists checks if a flag exists
   123→func (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, p storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {
   124→	var count int64
   125→
   126→	err := s.builder.Select("COUNT(*)").
   127→		From("flags").
   128→		Where(sq.Eq{"namespace_key": p.Namespace(), "\"key\"": p.Key}).
   129→		QueryRowContext(ctx).
   130→		Scan(&count)

Excellent! Let me create a summary of the changes I've made:

## Summary

I have successfully added the `FlagExists` method to the `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface and implemented it in all concrete types. Here's what was changed:

### 1. **Interface Definition** (`internal/storage/storage.go`)
Added the method signature to the `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface:
```go
FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req ResourceRequest) (bool, error)
```

### 2. **Snapshot Implementation** (`internal/storage/fs/snapshot.go`)
Implemented in-memory check for flag existence:
```go
func (ss *Snapshot) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {
    ns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())
    if err != nil {
        return false, err
    }
    _, ok := ns.flags[req.Key]
    return ok, nil
}
```

### 3. **Filesystem Store Implementation** (`internal/storage/fs/store.go`)
Delegates to the underlying snapshot store:
```go
func (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (exists bool, err error) {
    return exists, s.viewer.View(ctx, req.Reference, func(ss storage.ReadOnlyStore) error {
        exists, err = ss.FlagExists(ctx, req)
        return err
    })
}
```

### 4. **SQL Store Implementation** (`internal/storage/sql/common/flag.go`)
Uses an efficient COUNT query:
```go
func (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, p storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {
    var count int64
    err := s.builder.Select("COUNT(*)").
        From("flags").
        Where(sq.Eq{"namespace_key": p.Namespace(), "\"key\"": p.Key}).
        QueryRowContext(ctx).
        Scan(&count)
    if err != nil {
        return false, err
    }
    return count > 0, nil
}
```

provided\n// slice of paths resolved against the provided fs.FS.\nfunc SnapshotFromPaths(logger *zap.Logger, ffs fs.FS, paths []string, opts ...containers.Option[SnapshotOption]) (*Snapshot, error) nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfiles = append(files, fi)\n\t}\n\n\treturn SnapshotFromFiles(logger, files, opts...)\n}\n\n// SnapshotFromFiles constructs a StoreSnapshot from the provided slice\n// of fs.File implementations.\nfunc SnapshotFromFiles(logger *zap.Logger, files []fs.File, opts ...containers.Option[SnapshotOption]) (*Snapshot, error) {\n\tnow := flipt.Now()\n\ts := Snapshot{\n\t\tns: map[string]*namespace{\n\t\t\tdefaultNs: newNamespace(\"default\", \"Default\", now),\n\t\t},\n\t\tevalDists: map[string][]*storage.EvaluationDistribution{},\n\t\tnow:       now,\n\t}\n\n\tvar so SnapshotOption\n\tcontainers.ApplyAll(&so, opts...)\n\n\tfor _, fi := range files {\n\t\tdefer fi.Close()\n\t\tinfo, err := fi.Stat()\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tlogger.Debug(\"opening state file\", zap.String(\"path\", info.Name()))\n\n\t\tdocs, err := documentsFromFile(fi, so)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, doc := range docs {\n\t\t\tif err := s.addDoc(doc); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn &s, nil\n}\n\n// WalkDocuments walks all the Flipt feature documents found in the target fs.FS\n// based on either the default index file or an index file located in the root\nfunc WalkDocuments(logger *zap.Logger, src fs.FS, fn func(*ext.Document) error) error {\n\tpaths, err := listStateFiles(logger, src)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, file := range paths {\n\t\tlogger.Debug(\"opening state file\", zap.String(\"path\", file))\n\n\t\tfi, err := src.Open(file)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\tdefer fi.Close()\n\n\t\tdocs, err := documentsFromFile(fi, SnapshotOption{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, doc := range docs {\n\t\t\tif err := fn(doc); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// documentsFromFile parses and validates a document from a single fs.File instance\nfunc documentsFromFile(fi fs.File, opts SnapshotOption) ([]*ext.Document, error) {\n\tvalidator, err := validation.NewFeaturesValidator(opts.validatorOption...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tstat, err := fi.Stat()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tbuf := &bytes.Buffer{}\n\treader := io.TeeReader(fi, buf)\n\n\tvar docs []*ext.Document\n\textn := filepath.Ext(stat.Name())\n\n\tvar decode func(any) error\n\tswitch extn {\n\tcase \".yaml\", \".yml\":\n\t\t// Support YAML stream by looping until we reach an EOF.\n\t\tdecode = yaml.NewDecoder(buf).Decode\n\tcase \"\", \".json\":\n\t\tdecode = json.NewDecoder(buf).Decode\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected extension: %q\", extn)\n\t}\n\n\t// validate after we have checked supported\n\t// extensions but before we attempt to decode the\n\t// buffers contents to ensure we fill the buffer\n\t// via the TeeReader\n\tif err := validator.Validate(stat.Name(), reader); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tdoc := &ext.Document{}\n\t\tif err := decode(doc); err != nil {\n\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, io.EOF) {\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// set namespace to default if empty in document\n\t\tif doc.Namespace == \"\" {\n\t\t\tdoc.Namespace = \"default\"\n\t\t}\n\t\tdocs = append(docs, doc)\n\t}\n\n\treturn docs, nil\n}\n\n// listStateFiles lists all the file paths in a provided fs.FS containing Flipt feature state\nfunc listStateFiles(logger *zap.Logger, src fs.FS) ([]string, error) {\n\tidx, err := OpenFliptIndex(logger, src)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tvar paths []string\n\tif err := fs.WalkDir(src, \".\", func(path string, d fs.DirEntry, err error) error {\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif d.IsDir() {\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif idx.Match(path) {\n\t\t\tpaths = append(paths, path)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn paths, nil\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) addDoc(doc *ext.Document) error {\n\tns := ss.ns[doc.Namespace]\n\tif ns == nil {\n\t\tns = newNamespace(doc.Namespace, doc.Namespace, ss.now)\n\t}\n\n\tevalDists := map[string][]*storage.EvaluationDistribution{}\n\tif len(ss.evalDists) > 0 {\n\t\tevalDists = ss.evalDists\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, s := range doc.Segments {\n\t\tmatchType := flipt.MatchType_value[s.MatchType]\n\t\tsegment := &flipt.Segment{\n\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\tName:         s.Name,\n\t\t\tKey:          s.Key,\n\t\t\tDescription:  s.Description,\n\t\t\tMatchType:    flipt.MatchType(matchType),\n\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, constraint := range s.Constraints {\n\t\t\tconstraintType := flipt.ComparisonType_value[constraint.Type]\n\t\t\tsegment.Constraints = append(segment.Constraints, &flipt.Constraint{\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:   segment.Key,\n\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n\t\t\t\tOperator:     constraint.Operator,\n\t\t\t\tProperty:     constraint.Property,\n\t\t\t\tType:         flipt.ComparisonType(constraintType),\n\t\t\t\tValue:        constraint.Value,\n\t\t\t\tDescription:  constraint.Description,\n\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tns.segments[segment.Key] = segment\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, f := range doc.Flags {\n\t\tflagType := flipt.FlagType_value[f.Type]\n\t\tflag := &flipt.Flag{\n\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\tKey:          f.Key,\n\t\t\tName:         f.Name,\n\t\t\tDescription:  f.Description,\n\t\t\tEnabled:      f.Enabled,\n\t\t\tType:         flipt.FlagType(flagType),\n\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, v := range f.Variants {\n\t\t\tattachment, err := json.Marshal(v.Attachment)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tflag.Variants = append(flag.Variants, &flipt.Variant{\n\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\tKey:          v.Key,\n\t\t\t\tName:         v.Name,\n\t\t\t\tDescription:  v.Description,\n\t\t\t\tAttachment:   string(attachment),\n\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tns.flags[f.Key] = flag\n\n\t\tevalRules := []*storage.EvaluationRule{}\n\t\tfor i, r := range f.Rules {\n\t\t\trank := int32(i + 1)\n\t\t\trule := &flipt.Rule{\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      f.Key,\n\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tevalRule := &storage.EvaluationRule{\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      f.Key,\n\t\t\t\tID:           rule.Id,\n\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tswitch s := r.Segment.IsSegment.(type) {\n\t\t\tcase ext.SegmentKey:\n\t\t\t\trule.SegmentKey = string(s)\n\t\t\tcase *ext.Segments:\n\t\t\t\trule.SegmentKeys = s.Keys\n\t\t\t\tsegmentOperator := flipt.SegmentOperator_value[s.SegmentOperator]\n\n\t\t\t\trule.SegmentOperator = flipt.SegmentOperator(segmentOperator)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tvar (\n\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = []string{}\n\t\t\t\tsegments    = make(map[string]*storage.EvaluationSegment)\n\t\t\t)\n\n\t\t\tif rule.SegmentKey != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rule.SegmentKey)\n\t\t\t} else if len(rule.SegmentKeys) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rule.SegmentKeys...)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tfor _, segmentKey := range segmentKeys {\n\t\t\t\tsegment := ns.segments[segmentKey]\n\t\t\t\tif segment == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag %s/%s rule %d references unknown segment %q\", doc.Namespace, flag.Key, rank, segmentKey)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tevc := make([]storage.EvaluationConstraint, 0, len(segment.Constraints))\n\t\t\t\tfor _, constraint := range segment.Constraints {\n\t\t\t\t\tevc = append(evc, storage.EvaluationConstraint{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tOperator: constraint.Operator,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tProperty: constraint.Property,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tType:     constraint.Type,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tValue:    constraint.Value,\n\t\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tsegments[segmentKey] = &storage.EvaluationSegment{\n\t\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:  segmentKey,\n\t\t\t\t\tMatchType:   segment.MatchType,\n\t\t\t\t\tConstraints: evc,\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif rule.SegmentOperator == flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR {\n\t\t\t\tevalRule.SegmentOperator = flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tevalRule.Segments = segments\n\n\t\t\tevalRules = append(evalRules, evalRule)\n\n\t\t\tfor _, d := range r.Distributions {\n\t\t\t\tvariant, found := findByKey(d.VariantKey, flag.Variants...)\n\t\t\t\tif !found {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag %s/%s rule %d references unknown variant %q\", doc.Namespace, flag.Key, rank, d.VariantKey)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tid := uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String()\n\t\t\t\trule.Distributions = append(rule.Distributions, &flipt.Distribution{\n\t\t\t\t\tId:        id,\n\t\t\t\t\tRollout:   d.Rollout,\n\t\t\t\t\tRuleId:    rule.Id,\n\t\t\t\t\tVariantId: variant.Id,\n\t\t\t\t\tCreatedAt: ss.now,\n\t\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt: ss.now,\n\t\t\t\t})\n\n\t\t\t\tevalDists[evalRule.ID] = append(evalDists[evalRule.ID], &storage.EvaluationDistribution{\n\t\t\t\t\tID:                id,\n\t\t\t\t\tRollout:           d.Rollout,\n\t\t\t\t\tVariantID:         variant.Id,\n\t\t\t\t\tVariantKey:        variant.Key,\n\t\t\t\t\tVariantAttachment: variant.Attachment,\n\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tns.rules[rule.Id] = rule\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tns.evalRules[f.Key] = evalRules\n\n\t\tevalRollouts := make([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, 0, len(f.Rollouts))\n\t\tfor i, rollout := range f.Rollouts {\n\t\t\trank := int32(i + 1)\n\t\t\ts := &storage.EvaluationRollout{\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tflagRollout := &flipt.Rollout{\n\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      f.Key,\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif rollout.Threshold != nil {\n\t\t\t\ts.Threshold = &storage.RolloutThreshold{\n\t\t\t\t\tPercentage: rollout.Threshold.Percentage,\n\t\t\t\t\tValue:      rollout.Threshold.Value,\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\ts.RolloutType = flipt.RolloutType_THRESHOLD_ROLLOUT_TYPE\n\n\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Type = s.RolloutType\n\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Rule = &flipt.Rollout_Threshold{\n\t\t\t\t\tThreshold: &flipt.RolloutThreshold{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tPercentage: rollout.Threshold.Percentage,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tValue:      rollout.Threshold.Value,\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t} else if rollout.Segment != nil {\n\t\t\t\tvar (\n\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = []string{}\n\t\t\t\t\tsegments    = make(map[string]*storage.EvaluationSegment)\n\t\t\t\t)\n\n\t\t\t\tif rollout.Segment.Key != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rollout.Segment.Key)\n\t\t\t\t} else if len(rollout.Segment.Keys) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rollout.Segment.Keys...)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tfor _, segmentKey := range segmentKeys {\n\t\t\t\t\tsegment, ok := ns.segments[segmentKey]\n\t\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t\treturn errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag %s/%s rule %d references unknown segment %q\", doc.Namespace, flag.Key, rank, segmentKey)\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tconstraints := make([]storage.EvaluationConstraint, 0, len(segment.Constraints))\n\t\t\t\t\tfor _, c := range segment.Constraints {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tconstraints = append(constraints, storage.EvaluationConstraint{\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tOperator: c.Operator,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tProperty: c.Property,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tType:     c.Type,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tValue:    c.Value,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tsegments[segmentKey] = &storage.EvaluationSegment{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:  segmentKey,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tMatchType:   segment.MatchType,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tConstraints: constraints,\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tsegmentOperator := flipt.SegmentOperator_value[rollout.Segment.Operator]\n\n\t\t\t\ts.Segment = &storage.RolloutSegment{\n\t\t\t\t\tSegments:        segments,\n\t\t\t\t\tSegmentOperator: flipt.SegmentOperator(segmentOperator),\n\t\t\t\t\tValue:           rollout.Segment.Value,\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\ts.RolloutType = flipt.RolloutType_SEGMENT_ROLLOUT_TYPE\n\n\t\t\t\tfrs := &flipt.RolloutSegment{\n\t\t\t\t\tValue:           rollout.Segment.Value,\n\t\t\t\t\tSegmentOperator: flipt.SegmentOperator(segmentOperator),\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tif len(segmentKeys) == 1 {\n\t\t\t\t\tfrs.SegmentKey = segmentKeys[0]\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tfrs.SegmentKeys = segmentKeys\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Type = s.RolloutType\n\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Rule = &flipt.Rollout_Segment{\n\t\t\t\t\tSegment: frs,\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tns.rollouts[flagRollout.Id] = flagRollout\n\n\t\t\tevalRollouts = append(evalRollouts, s)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tns.evalRollouts[f.Key] = evalRollouts\n\t}\n\n\tss.ns[doc.Namespace] = ns\n\n\tss.evalDists = evalDists\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (ss Snapshot) String() string {\n\treturn \"snapshot\"\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) GetRule(ctx context.Context, p storage.NamespaceRequest, id string) (rule *flipt.Rule, _ error) {\n\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(p.Namespace())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tvar ok bool\n\trule, ok = ns.rules[id]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf(`rule \"%s/%s\"`, p.Namespace(), id)\n\t}\n\n\treturn rule, nil\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) ListRules(ctx context.Context, req *storage.ListRequest[storage.ResourceRequest]) (set storage.ResultSet[*flipt.Rule], _ error) {\n\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Predicate.Namespace())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn set, err\n\t}\n\n\trules := make([]*flipt.Rule, 0, len(ns.rules))\n\tfor _, rule := range ns.rules {\n\t\tif rule.FlagKey == req.Predicate.Key {\n\t\t\trules = append(rules, rule)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn paginate(req.QueryParams, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\treturn rules[i].Rank < rules[j].Rank\n\t}, rules...)\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) CountRules(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (uint64, error) {\n\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn 0, err\n\t}\n\n\tvar count uint64 = 0\n\tfor _, rule := range ns.rules {\n\t\tif rule.FlagKey == req.Key {\n\t\t\tcount += 1\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn count, nil\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) GetSegment(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Segment, error) {\n\tns, err := req)\n\t}\n\n\treturn segment, nil\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) ListSegments(ctx context.Context, req *storage.ListRequest[storage.NamespaceRequest]) (set storage.ResultSet[*flipt.Segment], err error) {\n\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Predicate.Namespace())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn set, err\n\t}\n\n\tsegments := make([]*flipt.Segment, 0, len(ns.segments))\n\tfor _, segment := range *Snapshot) CountSegments(ctx context.Context, p storage.NamespaceRequest) (uint64, error) {\n\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(p.Namespace())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn 0, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn uint64(len(ns.segments)), nil\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) GetNamespace(ctx context.Context, p storage.NamespaceRequest) (*flipt.Namespace, error) {\n\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(p.Namespace())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn ns.resource, nil\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) ListNamespaces(ctx context.Context, req *storage.ListRequest[storage.ReferenceRequest]) (set GetEvaluationRules(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRule, error) {\n\tns, ok := ss.ns[flag.Namespace()]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf(\"namespace %q\", flag.NamespaceRequest)\n\t}\n\n\trules, ok := ns.evalRules[flag.Key]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf(\"flag %q\", flag)\n\t}\n\n\treturn rules, ([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, error) {\n\tns, ok := ss.ns[flag.Namespace()]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf(\"namespace %q\", flag.NamespaceRequest)\n\t}\n\n\trollouts, ok := 1. EDIT /workspace/internal/storage/storage.go
Before
// ReadOnlyFlagStore supports retrieval of flags
type ReadOnlyFlagStore interface {
	GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error)
	ListFlags(ctx context.Context, req *ListRequest[NamespaceRequest]) (ResultSet[*flipt.Flag], error)
	CountFlags(ctx context.Context, ns NamespaceRequest) (uint64, error)
}
After
// ReadOnlyFlagStore supports retrieval of flags
type ReadOnlyFlagStore interface {
	GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error)
	FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req ResourceRequest) (bool, error)
	ListFlags(ctx context.Context, req *ListRequest[NamespaceRequest]) (ResultSet[*flipt.Flag], error)
	CountFlags(ctx context.Context, ns NamespaceRequest) (uint64, error)
}
2. EDIT /workspace/internal/storage/fs/snapshot.go
Before
func (ss *Snapshot) GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error) {
	ns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	flag, ok := ns.flags[req.Key]
	if !ok {
		return nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf("flag %q", req)
	}

	return flag, nil
}
After
func (ss *Snapshot) GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error) {
	ns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	flag, ok := ns.flags[req.Key]
	if !ok {
		return nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf("flag %q", req)
	}

	return flag, nil
}

func (ss *Snapshot) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {
	ns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())
	if err != nil {
		return false, err
	}

	_, ok := ns.flags[req.Key]
	return ok, nil
}
3. EDIT /workspace/internal/storage/fs/store.go
Before
func (s *Store) GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (flag *flipt.Flag, err error) {
	return flag, s.viewer.View(ctx, req.Reference, func(ss storage.ReadOnlyStore) error {
		flag, err = ss.GetFlag(ctx, req)
		return err
	})
}

func (s *Store) ListFlags(ctx context.Context, req *storage.ListRequest[storage.NamespaceRequest]) (set storage.ResultSet[*flipt.Flag], err error) {
After
func (s *Store) GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (flag *flipt.Flag, err error) {
	return flag, s.viewer.View(ctx, req.Reference, func(ss storage.ReadOnlyStore) error {
		flag, err = ss.GetFlag(ctx, req)
		return err
	})
}

func (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (exists bool, err error) {
	return exists, s.viewer.View(ctx, req.Reference, func(ss storage.ReadOnlyStore) error {
		exists, err = ss.FlagExists(ctx, req)
		return err
	})
}

// GetFlag gets a flag with variants by key
func (s *Store) GetFlag(ctx context.Context, p storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error) {
	var (
		createdAt fliptsql.Timestamp
		updatedAt fliptsql.Timestamp

		flag = &flipt.Flag{}

		err = s.builder.Select("namespace_key, \"key\", \"type\", name, description, enabled, created_at, updated_at").
			From("flags").
			Where(sq.Eq{"namespace_key": p.Namespace(), "\"key\"": p.Key}).
			QueryRowContext(ctx).
			Scan(
				&flag.NamespaceKey,
				&flag.Key,
				&flag.Type,
				&flag.Name,
				&flag.Description,
				&flag.Enabled,
				&createdAt,
				&updatedAt)
	)

		if errors.Is(err, sql.ErrNoRows) {
			return nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf("flag %q", p)
		}

		return nil, err
	}

	flag.UpdatedAt = updatedAt.Timestamp

Before
// FlagExists checks if a flag exists
func (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, p storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {
	var exists bool

	err := s.builder.Select("EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM flags WHERE namespace_key = ? AND \"key\" = ?)").
		From("flags").
		Where(sq.Eq{"namespace_key": p.Namespace(), "\"key\"": p.Key}).
		QueryRowContext(ctx).
		Scan(&exists)

	if err != nil {
		if errors.Is(err, sql.ErrNoRows) {
			return false, nil
		}
		return false, err
	}

	return exists, nil
}
After
// FlagExists checks if a flag exists
func (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, p storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {
	var count int64

	err := s.builder.Select("COUNT(*)").
		From("flags").
		Where(sq.Eq{"namespace_key": p.Namespace(), "\"key\"": p.Key}).
		QueryRowContext(ctx).
		Scan(&count)

	if err != nil {
		return false, err
	}

	return count > 0, nil
}
